   Begin Object Name="MaterialExpressionCustom_0" ExportPath="/Script/Engine.MaterialExpressionCustom'/Engine/Transient.PreviewMaterial_0:MaterialGraph_0.MaterialGraphNode_Custom_0.MaterialExpressionCustom_0'"
      Code="    // Dot product - the cosine of the angle between 2 vectors.\r\n\r\nfloat dot_prod = dot(q1, q2);\r\n    \r\n    // Clamp dot to [-1, 1] to handle floating-point precision issues.\r\n    dot_prod = clamp(dot_prod, -1.0, 1.0);\r\n    \r\n    // If the dot product is negative, slerp won\'t take\r\n    // the shorter path. Note that q1 and q2 are not normalized in this case.\r\n    if (dot_prod < 0.0f)\r\n    {\r\n        q1 = -q1;\r\n        dot_prod = -dot_prod;\r\n    }\r\n\r\n    // If angle == 0.0, just return one input.\r\n    if (dot_prod >= 1.0)\r\n    {\r\n        return q1;\r\n    }\r\n\r\n    // Calculate the angle between the quaternions.\r\n    float theta = acos(dot_prod);\r\n    \r\n    // Calculate the sine of the angle.\r\n    float sinTheta = sin(theta);\r\n    \r\n    // If sinTheta is close to zero, use linear interpolation instead.\r\n    if (sinTheta < 0.001)\r\n    {\r\n        return normalize((1.0 - t) * q1 + t * q2);\r\n    }\r\n    \r\n    // Calculate the interpolation weights.\r\n    float w1 = sin((1.0 - t) * theta) / sinTheta;\r\n    float w2 = sin(t * theta) / sinTheta;\r\n    \r\n    // Interpolate and return the result.\r\n    return w1 * q1 + w2 * q2;\r\n"
      OutputType=CMOT_Float4
      Inputs(0)=(InputName="q1",Input=(Expression="/Script/Engine.MaterialExpressionTextureSample'MaterialGraphNode_59.MaterialExpressionTextureSample_0'",OutputIndex=5,Mask=1,MaskR=1,MaskG=1,MaskB=1,MaskA=1))
